Problem of New Special Police Rotation in the War Zone 101

Yi Wo and Chaisan Came to Tianjin to Discuss

Must Wait for Meeting to Resolve

Tianjin Communication, Yi Wo, Chief of the Japanese Military Affairs Office in Shanhaiguan, came to Tianjin from Beiping on the 20th and met with Meijiro Umezu, commander of the Japanese army in Tianjin, to exchange views on the rotation of our newly compiled war zone special police force to the east. At noon on the 21st, Kenjiro Chaisan also rushed over from Beiping and visited Umezu with Yi Wo to discuss the matter. At 4:00 PM that afternoon, Chaisan, accompanied by Tanaka, deputy consul of the Japanese consulate in Tianjin, went to the provincial government to visit Gan Xuezhong to discuss this issue. It has been generally decided that the only difference is that the Japanese side wants the date for the eastern rotation of our newly compiled special police force to be implemented without further discussion, and the number of personnel must comply with the regulations of 6,000. Each company of light machine guns is only allowed to carry four. The location of their garrison must also not differ from the area where the current security team is stationed. Before entering the war zone, representatives of the Kwantung Army and the North China Garrison Army must send personnel to check to avoid exceeding the agreed number of personnel and carrying too many light machine guns. The provincial government believes that reducing the number of light machine guns is tantamount to reducing the strength of the team. Bandits in various parts of the war zone are rising up, and without more powerful firearms, how can they be suppressed? Therefore, they do not quite agree. Chaisan returned to Beiping on the afternoon of the 22nd, and Yi Wo went to Beiping again on the 23rd. He will invite members of our war zone cleaning committee Zhu Shiqin, Yin Rugeng, Yin Tong, and Xu Shen to hold a meeting in Beiping on the 26th and 27th to discuss and decide. According to this observation, the eastern opening of the new special warfare team may only be realized after the new year.

Regarding the handover of Malanyu Eastern Tombs, Yi Wo, who came to Tianjin, said that he had met with Yin Rugeng many times and that the handover was not a problem. It can be realized soon. The order of handover in the future is to hand over Malanyu first and then the Eastern Tombs. This time, Yi Wo will go to Beiping again to discuss this matter with Yin Rugeng in addition to discussing the rotation of the special police team into the war zone.

Regarding the problem of reorganizing the Yutian war zone security supplementary team, the Japanese side hopes that we will increase the number of personnel to 2,000 according to the organizational structure of Liu Ren's regiment and Zhao Lei's department of the war zone security first and second brigades, and transfer them out of Yutian so that the people can rest and county administration can be promoted. Their new defense area is Qinhuangdao. Zhu Shiqin went to Yutian a few days ago to contact the leaders of the team, and there were no objections. However, the method has not yet been realized. On the 21st of this month, the team suddenly clashed again with the Wang Jizong department of the militia in Yagongqiao Town, firing guns all night. The residents were panicked, and many people fled to other counties one after another and were looted and shot by the team on the way. The Cleaning Committee then sent Zhu Shiqin to mediate again. Zhu arrived in Yutian on the 22nd and is currently mediating. Chairman Yu Xuezhong of Hebei Province believes that the security team is undisciplined and wreaks havoc on the area, and regardless of where they are transferred, they cannot be peaceful, so he is still considering the matter of going to Qinhuangdao. (23rd)

Nindu Holds Memorial Service for the Third Route Army 102

Representatives of the Worshippers Depart from Nanchang

Xiong Shihui and Others Smoothly Inspect Recovered Areas

Nanchang Communication, The memorial service for the officers and soldiers of the Third Route Army who died in the suppression of bandits is scheduled to be held on the 25th at Nindufangci. Chairman Lin of the National Government, Representative Xiong Shihui, and other central representatives, representatives of the various route army divisions, representatives of various mass organizations, officials of the provincial capital, etc., a total of more than 100 people, took 22 cars on the 23rd, gathered at Pinganbao outside Shunwai, led by two armored vehicles in front, and escorted by a platoon of guards from the Xingying and Provincial Government in seven large cars. They set off at 9:00 AM and arrived at Linchuan at 11:00 AM. After lunch in Nancheng, they stayed overnight in Nanfeng and were able to reach Nindu on the morning of the 24th. The details are described as follows:

Origin of the Assembly 103

The Jiangxi bandit suppression military affairs progressed rapidly under the personal supervision of Chairman Chiang. The war was fierce, and the number of deaths and injuries was the highest. The Nanchang, Baishe, Ganzhu, Guangchang, Baishuizhen, Yiqian, Nindu, and other battles were all on the Third Route Army's offensive line. Now that the bandit suppression military affairs have come to an end, Chen Cheng, commander-in-chief of the route, in order to pay tribute to the officers and soldiers who died in battle and to the great merits of sacrificing themselves for the country and the people, initiated a memorial service in Nindu to comfort the loyal souls, and invited important party and state figures and people from all walks of life to participate. Luo Zhuoying, the deputy commander-in-chief of the route, is in charge of everything in Nindu.

Important Persons Involved 104

The central authorities, in order to sympathize with the officers and soldiers who bravely followed orders in the bandit suppression, either appointed representatives or participated in person. Chairman Lin of the National Government sent Chairman Xiong of the Provincial Government, Chairman Chiang of the Military Affairs Commission sent President Chen of the Military Advisory Yuan, President Wang of the Executive Yuan sent Director Peng of the Political Affairs Department, Commander Chen of the Southern Route Bandit Suppression Army sent representative Li Shangyong, Zhang Fang, Commander-in-Chief of the 20th Route, Overseas Chinese Commissioners Lin Zechen and Ma Lisan represented Overseas Chinese, Cai Jinjun, Director of the General Affairs Department of the Nanchang Headquarters, Nie Xi, Deputy Director of the Second Division of the First Department, Yu Baiqing, a member of the Provincial Party Department, Cheng Shihui and Gong Xuesui, members of the Provincial Government, representatives of various armies and divisions, representatives of various mass organizations, and reporters from the Central News Agency, etc., more than 100 people.

Departure by Different Routes 105

The representatives and others departed from the province in three routes. The first route gathered at the Nanchang Office of the Third Route Army in Kuaizi Lane. The representatives of various armies and divisions and various mass organizations were invited by the office and carried dozens of flower wreaths, more than a dozen sacrificial texts, etc., donated by Chairman Chiang and various dignitaries, various armies and divisions, various agencies, and various groups, and took a car at 8:00 AM to go to the meeting point outside Shunwai first. The second route gathered in front of the gate of the General Headquarters, consisting of officers of the General Headquarters, Commissioner Yu of the Provincial Party Department, and the special team of the General Headquarters, and continued on at 8:30 AM. The third route gathered in front of Chairman Xiong's mansion at Lingying Bridge, consisting of Chairman Xiong, President Chen, Commander Zhang, Li Shangyong, Lin Zechen, etc., and 20 guards from the Provincial Government, taking 14 cars of various sizes and departing at 9:00 AM. The people from the various routes met at Pinganbao outside Shunwai at 10:00 AM and then headed south, led by armored vehicles. It was just after the light rain stopped, and the weather was clear.

Conversation Before Departure 106

Before the Central News Agency reporter and various representatives boarded the car and set off, they had brief conversations with the representatives. Chairman Xiong said, "In addition to being ordered to represent Chairman Lin in participating in this memorial service, I will also take the opportunity to inspect the post-disaster work in the newly recovered counties and give guidance to the county administration. The time will not be delayed for too long, and I will return to the province before the end of the year." Director Peng, representing President Wang, said, "This time, I was ordered to participate in the memorial service specifically. I originally planned to return to my hometown, but because my hometown of Anfu is not adjacent to Nindu and the time is suddenly short, I am afraid I will not be able to fulfill my wish." The two Directors Cheng and Gong requested to participate in the conference and then follow the chairman to inspect the county administration, paying special attention to special education and various constructions.

Overnight Stay in Nanfeng 107

According to the Central News Agency Nanfeng telephone on the 23rd, a group of more than 100 representatives attending the Third Route Army memorial service departed from the province at about 9:00 AM on the 23rd, passed through Linchuan at about 11:00 AM, arrived in Nancheng at 1:00 PM, and had lunch at Chairman Chiang's headquarters. They arrived in Nanfeng at 4:00 PM. Army Commander Mao Bingwen and County Magistrate Liu Qianjun led the boys and girls scouts and the Communist Elimination Volunteers to welcome them in the suburbs. Xiong Peng and others all went to the county government to rest, and the others stayed at the New Life Hotel. Han Wenyuan, Chief of Staff of the Third Route Army, had already come to Nanfeng from Nindu to greet them. Army Commander Mao then invited Xiong and others to cross the Fu River to visit Zhongshan Pavilion and inspect the bandit suppression relics. Chairman Xiong also briefly discussed the plan to dredge the Fu River with Director Gong at that place. After returning to the city, he returned to pay homage to Army Commander Mao, who prepared dinner and received Hu Jiazhao, Director of the Highway Office. They stayed overnight in Nanfeng and are scheduled to depart from Nanfeng at 8:00 AM on the morning of the 24th. It is 240 miles from Nan to Nindu, and it is estimated that they will arrive at 3:00 PM. The memorial service preparation office plans to guide them to visit Cuiwei Peak after Xiong and others arrive in Nindu. If the time is too late, they will wait until after the conference on the 25th to go again. (Central News Agency)

Qing Dynasty Royal Treasure: Dragon Eye Pearl Also for Sale 108

Said to Have the Effect of Prolonging Life

Buyer Also an American Merchant

(North Beiping Correspondence) Since the fall of the Manchu Qing dynasty, treasures from the palace have been disappearing one after another. After Puyi's sister-in-law, Pu Tang Shixia, secretly sold the Dust-Repelling Pearl to an American merchant, a person familiar with the Qing court recently revealed that the Qing Palace also possessed a Fire-Repelling Pearl and a Dragon Eye Pearl, each one, which have also been sold to an American. According to reports, "On the throne in the Qianqing Palace of the Qing Dynasty, there was a dragon head frame, with the Fire-Repelling Pearl embedded in its left eye and the Dust-Repelling Pearl in its right eye. The Fire-Repelling Pearl was lost during the Tongzhi and Guangxu eras. It is said that the Fire-Repelling Pearl was about the same size as the Dust-Repelling Pearl, with a black color and dazzling brilliance. If the pearl was placed in a tray, any candle lit within a foot of the pearl would extinguish without wind. As for the Dust-Repelling Pearl, it was removed by Puyi when he left the palace and placed on a table in the main hall. During the night, even with strong winds, the area within a foot of the pearl remained dust-free by the next morning. It was truly a supreme treasure."

It was also said that during the early Qing dynasty, when Vietnam paid tribute, they offered a Pearl of Longevity, also known as the Dragon Eye Pearl. The pearl was yellow with a black spot in the middle, resembling a dragon's eye, hence the name. It weighed about 1.8 qian (approx. 6.7 grams). In the early Qing dynasty, when Prince Regent Dorgon was in power, the Qing court bestowed this pearl as a reward. After Dorgon's death, his descendants regarded it as a family heirloom, storing it in a brocade pouch and wearing it on their navel, remaining free from illness throughout the year, indeed having the effect of prolonging life. Therefore, several generations of the Prince Rui lived to be eighty, ninety, or even a hundred years old. The pearl was warm in winter and cool in summer. Besides increasing lifespan, it was also rumored to have the ability to ward off weapons, fire, and water, which is quite absurd and not to be believed. The descendants of Prince Rui, after 1919 and 1920, experienced a decline in their family fortunes and decided to sell the pearl. After appraisal by Belgian and French jewelers, it was valued at 120,000 (currency not specified). The descendants of Prince Rui believed the pearl to be priceless and did not immediately sell it. Later, they used it as collateral to borrow 50,000 yuan from an American bank in Tianjin for a five-year term. A few years ago, they tried to sell it again, but the deal fell through due to a large difference in the price. It is now heard that the mortgage term for this pearl has expired, and those aware of the matter say that the descendants of the Prince, unable to redeem it, have sold it to the American bank for a price of 80,000 (currency not specified). It has now been shipped to the United States. The outflow of national treasures is truly regrettable. (23rd)

Taicang 109

Resignation of the Head of Shatou Town

The administrative region of Taicang County is currently divided into six districts. Shatou Town, which is under the county's jurisdiction, is the fifth district. The town head is enthusiastic in his work, but his straightforward nature inevitably makes him a target of jealousy. Recently, a certain newspaper in the county has used the town head as a target for attack. The town head, provoked by this, has become extremely passive in his attitude. He has previously resigned several times without success. This time, he may suddenly retire. However, there are many vying for the position of town head, and it remains to be seen who will ultimately succeed.

Wuxi 110

Main Culprit in Bribery and Release of Drug Dealer Arrested

Wu Liansheng (also known as Lian Suozi), an inspector from the Jiangyin County Drug Investigation Office, on July 11th of last year, apprehended Pan Renmei, who was using red pills, at the home of Lian Jisheng at No. 1 Huaishu Lane in Wuxi city. He extorted a large sum of money. Around October, Wu fled to Jiangyin and, together with Wu Bingjun, the former head of the Second Public Security Bureau of the county, seized red pills at the home of Chen Jinhe in Xiaoqingyang. They accepted a bribe of over 1,000 yuan to settle the matter privately. When the case was exposed, Wu and others fled without a trace. Both Wuxi and Jiangyin counties issued arrest warrants. Recently, Wu Liansheng, believing the situation had calmed down, secretly returned home and hid next to the Housheng Silk Factory in Nancangmen. Wu Rongquan, nicknamed "Zhonggangpen," discovered this and immediately instructed his friend Qian Shiliang to report it to the Second Public Security Bureau in charge. Director Gao of the bureau, upon receiving the report, immediately dispatched police chief Guan Shihao to arrest Wu Liansheng and brought him to the bureau for detention before transferring him to the General Bureau. Yesterday, he was transferred to the local branch court for interrogation. After the prosecutor, Ren, held a court hearing, he immediately ordered him to be detained pending judgment. At the same time, the Jiangyin County Party Headquarters, upon learning that Wu Liansheng, the fugitive who bribed and released Chen Jinhe, had been arrested, sent an official letter to the Jiangyin County Government, which was then forwarded to the local court, proposing to bring the suspect to Jiangyin for interrogation and trial.

Fires Occur One After Another 111

Fires have been occurring frequently in both urban and rural areas this month. The cause is mostly due to carelessness with fire. Yesterday alone, three fires occurred, resulting in significant losses. The details are as follows: (1) Zhou Qiantai Hat and Shoe Store, located at the northern end of Datie Bridge in the city, is owned by Zhou Weiquan from Wangting and also sells Weixu incense, embroidery, and other items. The business was doing quite well. Yesterday (25th) morning around 2:00 AM, a fire suddenly broke out on the second floor due to carelessness, with flames shooting out and breaking through the roof. The owner, Zhou Weiquan, and others, who lived on the third floor, jumped out of the windows and fled to the roof of the neighboring Meixin Incense and Powder Shop before managing to escape safely. As the fire intensified, and with the narrow streets, the windows of the Maolun Xiecheng Yong silk shops across the street were also affected. Fortunately, they used their own water pumps and exerted their efforts to extinguish the fire, thus preserving them, with only slight losses. Fire engines from Sections 1, 2, and 3 of the Central District also arrived at the scene upon hearing the alarm to extinguish the fire. As a result, Zhou Qiantai was mostly burned down, and although Meixin was not completely affected, the goods were water damaged. The combined losses for both families are estimated at three to four thousand yuan. (2) Two thatched huts in the rice fields near the Dade Bridge on Wuli Street outside the West Gate also caught fire last night due to carelessness. The Huishan and other fire brigades arrived at the scene to extinguish the fire. The two thatched huts were completely destroyed. Chen Heshang, a member of the Section 3 fire brigade in the Northern District, was injured in his right instep and buttocks by a fire engine while rushing to put out the fire. He was immediately sent to the Brothers Hospital for treatment. (3) A grass shed opposite the Yongtai Silk Factory outside the South Gate was also burned down last night, with only minor losses.

Changzhou 112

Scheduled Damming of the Wujin Section of the Canal

The Jiangsu Provincial Government is dredging the canal between Zhenjiang and Wujin as a form of work relief. The Wujin County Chamber of Commerce, based on letters from various trade associations, requested that the damming of the Wujin section of the canal be postponed, as the end of the year is approaching, and business relies heavily on water transport. The Chamber of Commerce immediately wrote to Chen Ziding, the director of the engineering office, requesting a postponement. Yesterday (24th), they received a reply stating that according to the original plan, all sections would be dammed simultaneously, and the area around Benniu in Wujin should have already been implemented. Considering the impact on business transport, it has already been postponed repeatedly. To take into account the difficulties of businesses, they are requested to notify all trades to complete the transfer of goods by the end of this month, under the premise of not hindering the dam construction, and the damming will begin at the beginning of next month, etc.

Inspection by the Head of the Security Department in Changzhou 113

Xiang Zhizhuang, the head of the Jiangsu Provincial Security Department and standing committee member of the Provincial Anti-Smoking Association, arrived in Changzhou today (25th) from Wuxi, accompanied by training supervisor Bai Zhujun and others, to inspect the security force and inspect the County Anti-Smoking Committee. County Magistrate Hou, upon hearing the news, had already gathered the security force in advance for an immediate assembly and inspection.

Zhenjiang 114

Prohibition of Villagers from Gathering to Stop Vehicles

The Jiangsu Construction Department believes that the long-distance bus company's vehicles are primarily intended to facilitate public transportation. Although it is a business venture, it is also beneficial to the public. In principle, the company and the public should have a mutual relationship of mutual benefit and reliance, and there should be no cause for hostility. However, there are often one or two cunning individuals who harbor personal grievances and either let livestock loose, damage trees, or allow their children to damage bridges, hindering traffic. Once the company intervenes, or the vehicles accidentally collide with livestock, they use this as an excuse to incite ignorant people to stop the vehicles. If someone is unfortunately injured in a collision, it becomes even more difficult to reason with them. To eliminate danger, a special request has been submitted to the province to instruct all counties to announce to the villagers that if long-distance buses have any unfortunate accidents, they can file a complaint with the government for a resolution in accordance with the law. They are not allowed to gather and stop vehicles, causing trouble.

Yangzhou 115

Suspicious Bandit Boat Discovered in Xianzhen

The home of Chen Jingan, a farmer in Renjia Bridge, Guihua Township, Second District of the county, was robbed of leather clothing and other items by bandits on the night of the 29th of last month. A report was filed with the county bureau for investigation. The anti-crime squad leader, Zhang Qingan, led police to Xianzhen the night before and discovered a small boat with suspicious movements. The boat dweller, Qiu Youde, and the five suspicious individuals, Xu Mingren, Shen Linan, Shen Rongzhu, and Shen Rongli, were all taken to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation. It is rumored to be related to the Chen robbery case.

Liyang Business Tax Bureau Forcibly Seizes Stores, Leading to a Strike 116

Liyang County suffered the most severe drought in the Jiangnan region this summer. Disaster victims were everywhere, and the commercial market plummeted. Shops were desolate, barely surviving, and still struggling to stay afloat. Unexpectedly, Zhou Yulin, the head of the Business Tax Bureau, disregarded the hardships faced by businesses. The stores were unable to pay the business taxes for the autumn and winter seasons in time. The bureau head believed that the merchants were intentionally resisting taxes. Without prior consultation, he suddenly dispatched police to the Tiancheng, Tianxiang, Derun, and other stores on Ximen Avenue at 11:00 AM yesterday (23rd), ordering them to close down and posting prepared notices at any time. He also sent the managers of these stores to the County Government for detention. As a result, all trade associations of the city's stores convened an emergency meeting, unanimously stating that this year's rare drought made it impossible for merchants to raise tax funds in time, not that they intentionally resisted taxes. The bureau head's actions were considered too erratic, and at 1:00 PM, all the stores went on strike. The County Chamber of Commerce immediately held a meeting, deciding to first telegraph the situation to the Civil Affairs and Finance Departments. This morning (24th), the various trade associations and the County Chamber of Commerce held another meeting, with County Magistrate Chen also attending, explaining the misunderstanding and hoping that the stores would resume business at any time. Representatives of the merchants and the standing committee of the Chamber of Commerce requested that the province send someone to Liyang to collect taxes and that the bureau head, Zhou Yulin, be dismissed. County Magistrate Chen did not give a specific answer, and the meeting ended without a resolution.

Xiaoshan 119

Disaster Victims Form Begging Group

The third district of Xiaoshan is located in Cexiang. The drought this summer was particularly severe. Although the province and county distributed buckwheat seeds, financial resources were exhausted, and people were unable to make a living. They could not even afford meals and mostly subsisted on bran, turnips, green weeds, and wild fruits. The strong have already considered desperate measures, while the weak have pawned everything, even selling their daughters and children, and some have even committed suicide. The situation is so dire that it brings tears to one's eyes. If assistance is not provided urgently, it may lead to disaster. It is heard that the province has allocated 170,000 (currency not specified) for work relief, which has been used for dredging the Nansha Canal, but it has not reached the southern region. Gentry in the city have jointly appealed to the provincial and county governments for relief. It is now heard that the disaster victims in the district have formed a begging group, and have been kneeling to government authorities to plead for assistance.

Yesterday Morning's Yunnan Uprising Commemoration 120

Xing Wan, a member of the Municipal Party Committee, presided over the meeting, reporting on the significance of the commemoration. The meeting adjourned at 11:00 AM. The details are as follows:

Assembly Order 121

(1) All stand at attention; (2) Sing the Party song; (3) Pay the highest respect to the Party and National Flag and the portrait of the General; (4) Read the General's will respectfully; (5) Moment of silence; (6) Report; (7) Speech; (8) Shout slogans; (9) Ceremony completed, adjournment.

Attending Representatives 122

Bao Jiasheng from the First District Paper Industry Union, Wang Zongjian from the Jianghai Customs Superintendency, Huang Zaoxiong from the Municipal Education Association, Hu Xiongding from Jiaotong University, Lin Keming from the Municipal Women's Association, Ren Bin from the Bone Ware Industry Union, Dong Chongmen from the Second Branch of the Jiangsu Higher Court, Huang Xianggu from the Second Special District Citizens' Federation, Zhu Xuefan from the General Labor Union, Yu Yaoqiu from the Native Products Industry Union, He Yuanming from the Accountants' Association, Zhu Ya Kui from the Labor Education Association, Lu Hongru from Shanghai University, and all staff members of the Municipal Party Headquarters, totaling over one hundred people.

Chairman's Report 123

After the formalities, Chairman Xing Wan delivered a report, stating that the Yunnan Uprising occurred because Yuan Shikai disregarded public opinion, acted arbitrarily, and declared himself emperor. Therefore, Mr. Cai Songpo, Mr. Tang Jiyao, and others launched the uprising in Yunnan and raised troops to punish Yuan. Various provinces responded. Yuan's betrayal of the Republic of China had been brewing for a long time. After the Xinhai Revolution, the General left the post of President and relinquished it to Yuan Shikai because many comrades in the Party misunderstood the success of the revolution, believing that the overthrow of the Qing Dynasty and the establishment of the Republic of China meant the success of the revolution. The General reorganized the Kuomintang into the Chinese Revolutionary Party to make the comrades aware that the revolutionary work of our party had not yet ended and still needed effort. The General once wrote to comrades in Nanyang, overseas branches, and Mr. Deng Zeru, stating that comrades should obey the party leader and strive for revolution. Unexpectedly, Yuan Shikai abandoned the provisional constitution, dissolved the parliament, and declared himself emperor. The General said that all internal wars in Chinese history had started with the declaration of an emperor. Today, our revolution aims to separate power and ability, with power belonging to the people and ability belonging to the government. The government is an omnipotent government, and the people are empowered people. The General has explained this in detail in the chapter on the Principle of Democracy. However, the foundation of democracy lies in the successful implementation of local autonomy. We can conclude that the success of the revolution requires (1) comrades to absolutely obey the party leader; (2) to absolutely obey the revolutionary strategy of the Three Principles of the People; and (3) to establish an omnipotent government.

Commemorative Slogans 124

(1) Promote the spirit of the Yunnan Uprising; (2) Cultivate democratic forces; (3) Eliminate feudal forces; (4) Thoroughly eliminate the Red bandits; (5) Actively develop the Northwest; (6) Recover lost territory in the Northeast; (7) Long live the Kuomintang; (8) Long live the Republic of China.

Ministry of Finance Considering Rewarding Silver Imports 126

Foreign Banks May Bring Silver Back to Shanghai

(Shen Shi News Agency) It is said that the banking industry in Shanghai has suggested that the Ministry of Finance reward silver imports. A reporter from Shen Shi News Agency learned from the banking industry yesterday that regarding the issue of rewarding silver imports, foreign businesses must request the government to refund the silver tax and equalization tax paid when the silver was previously exported, or to exempt the returned silver from export tax and equalization tax in the future. Only then would they be willing to bring silver back. This matter is related to the credibility of our government, and the Ministry of Finance is carefully considering whether to easily approve it. However, it is certain that leaders of the local banking industry and financial authorities have been discussing a proper solution for days. As for the rumor yesterday that HSBC Bank had remitted 20 million yuan from Hong Kong, this rumor has not been confirmed. Because the equalization tax and silver tax issues have not been resolved, it is not easy to bring back large amounts of silver. However, it is generally believed that it is indeed possible for HSBC Bank to bring back silver within a certain period. About two months ago, no less than 70 million yuan was transferred from Shanghai to Hong Kong. Previously, the cash crunch in Shantou and other places was severe, and HSBC issued more banknotes in South China. Therefore, to enhance its reserves, it had to collect a large amount of cash in Hong Kong to secure its credit. Now that the cash crunch has passed, it is indeed possible to transfer some of the cash in Hong Kong back to Shanghai.

Straits Settlements Restricting Our Cotton Textiles 128

International Trade Bureau Notifies Domestic Goods Groups to Pay Attention

The International Trade Bureau recently received a report from the Consulate in Penang, stating that the Straits Settlements government gazetted the import quota restrictions for foreign cotton textiles in 1935. The restriction quota for our country next year is 12,190,559 yards: 800,051 yards of bleached cotton cloth, 10,145,075 yards of dyed cotton cloth, 236,184 yards of printed cloth, 1,468 yards of woolen colored cloth, 292 yards of cotton sarong cloth, 1,005,321 yards of artificial silk (not yarn or cloth), and 28 yards of artificial silk yarn or cloth, totaling 12,190,559 yards. This is of great importance to the future of our country's cotton textile exports. The bureau has now notified the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the China National Products Production and Sales Federation, the Shanghai Machine Weaving National Products Factory Federation, and other domestic goods groups to inform all cotton textile exporters to pay attention.

Shanghai West National Products Exhibition Closed Yesterday 129

Citizens Enthusiastically Purchased Goods, Results Quite Good

Plans to Hold National Products Exhibitions in East and North Shanghai

The second Shanghai West National Products Exhibition, sponsored by the Shanghai Citizens' National Products Promotion Association, closed yesterday after being open for three weeks. Striving to Stabilize Shanghai's Financial Market 131

Stabilizing Finances 132

Famine Relief Association 142

Large Batch of Relief Personnel Dispatched

First to Anhui, Jiangxi and Six Other Provinces for Inspection and Relief

Inspection and Relief Not Passing Through the Hands of Others

The Shanghai Famine Relief Association for Various Provinces held a meeting the other day to allocate relief funds to various provinces, and after assigning personnel to investigate and distribute the relief, today the investigation and distribution personnel assigned by the association have set off to the disaster areas of various provinces. In addition, the Famine Relief Association is also carrying out relief work with rice, flour and winter clothing. Details are recorded as follows:

Distribution of Relief Funds 143

The Famine Relief Association has determined that there are as many as 19 provinces affected by drought this year and plans to distribute relief funds of 30 million yuan. The most severely affected provinces are Anhui, Jiangxi, Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Hunan, and Hubei. Among these six provinces, Jiangsu, which is less severely affected, will receive a relief fund of 40,000 yuan, while the others will receive 80,000 yuan. These relief funds have been borrowed from the banking sector by the authorities of the Famine Relief Association, and the donated funds will be used to repay the loans, which has been negotiated. After the investigation and distribution personnel go to various provinces, they can send telegrams at any time, and the banks in Shanghai will allocate and remit the funds to the disaster areas for distribution.

Personnel Dispatched 144

After the investigation and distribution personnel for the first six provinces were decided, all provinces have been urgently urging them by telegram, as the winter is approaching. Therefore, the investigation and distribution personnel for each province are scheduled to set off to the disaster areas of each province in succession. Those who have already left Shanghai today include Hong San and Zhang Zepu, who are going to Anhui Province for investigation and distribution, and left Shanghai on the Jiangshun wheel. In addition, Qu Wenliu, who is going to Zhejiang, Li Dixian, who is going to Jiangxi, He Hengfu, who is going to Hubei, Zhao Yiwu, who is going to Hunan, and Zhang Lanping, who is going to Jiangsu, will all leave Shanghai in succession within days.

Relief Method 145

The Famine Relief Association will provide cash for the investigation and distribution in the first six provinces. The procedure is that after the investigation and distribution personnel arrive in the disaster area, they will conduct on-site investigations and consider the severity of the disaster and the amount of relief needed, and then telegraph Shanghai to allocate and remit the funds. The distribution of relief funds will also be presided over by the investigation and distribution personnel, and will not pass through the hands of others, so as to ensure that the disaster victims receive practical benefits. In addition, the association is also in great need of rice, flour, and winter clothing. The 100,000 stones of foreign rice that were previously planned to be purchased has been decided to be changed to domestic rice. The flour has been handed over to the Ningbo Fellow Villagers Association for relief, and the winter clothing is all being packed.

Huang Shaoxiong's Telegram 146

Huang Shaoxiong, the newly appointed chairman of Zhejiang, sent a telegram to the Famine Relief Association yesterday, expressing his gratitude for the 80,000 yuan in relief aid on behalf of the disaster victims. The original telegram read: "Chairman Kong of the Famine Relief Association for Various Provinces, and to vice chairmen Xu and Wang: I have received your telegram with respect. I am grateful that you have decided to allocate 80,000 yuan in relief funds to our province. Your benevolence and kindness, and your gift of food and clothing to the hungry and cold, I respectfully thank you on behalf of the disaster victims of the entire province. Huang Shaoxiong, respectfully."

Chen Jian'an and Others Raise Money for Zhejiang Relief 149

To be Handled Together with Mr. Luo Qinghua

Chen Jian'an, Deputy Governor of the Central Bank, and Luo Qinghua, Deputy Manager of the Silk Bank, are both natives of Zhuji, Zhejiang. Both men are deeply saddened by the fact that their hometown, Zhuji, has suffered a severe drought this year, with no grain harvested, and the disaster victims in various districts are eating tree bark and grass roots, and the starving are everywhere. Moreover, with the approach of winter, bandits are everywhere, and the people cannot sleep peacefully. Yesterday, both men received a report from the Zhuji County Branch of the Zhejiang Relief Association, which read as follows: "We understand that Zhuji County has suffered an unprecedented drought, with almost all the agricultural products destroyed. Hundreds of thousands of disaster victims are waiting to be fed and clothed. With the approach of winter, they are suffering from hunger and cold, and their livelihoods have been cut off. Recently, the disaster victims in the fifth, seventh, and eighth districts, which are the most severely affected, are using tree bark and grass roots to fill their hunger. Many have been without food for several days and have not been able to cook. Some have even been unable to find food, and the starving are everywhere. The reports sent to you about the disaster in Zhuji are all true. The members of our association in the county are heartbroken. After a regular meeting, we decided to raise 2,000 yuan to purchase 304 stones of corn, and distribute it proportionally according to the severity of the disaster in the fifth, seventh, and eighth districts. The fifth district will receive 106.6 dou, the seventh district will receive 122.2 dou, and the eighth district will receive 75.4 dou. We have invited Mr. Shen Peian of the Jisheng Branch to send personnel to the disaster-stricken villages of Meilei, Yuanbi, Xinqi, Tangren, Chayuan, Nanyuan, Xiyuan, and Pingshan in the fifth district (Shangnan), Shangyu, Shanghe, Chengshan, Xitai, and Changai in the seventh district (Daxi), and Pudai, Minyi, and Zhangcun in the eighth district (Xiaoxi), to select the truly helpless and distribute the corn to them. The relief grain is the best we can do, and the amount received by the disaster victims is very small. It is truly a drop in the bucket and cannot solve the problem. This is a summary of the recent emergency relief work of our association. However, hundreds of thousands of disaster victims in the county are eagerly awaiting relief, and the situation is urgent. We have no resources to start with, and the members of our association are worried and anxious, and have no way to provide relief. We hope that you will do your best to raise money, and appeal to the National Relief Association and the Jiasu Relief Association for relief. The more, the better, and the sooner, the better, so as to save the disaster victims and give them a chance to start a new life."

All-Zhejiang Association Sends a Telegram to Chairman Huang of Zhejiang Province 154

Please Reduce the Special Construction Donation in Accordance with the Ministry's Consultation

The All-Zhejiang Association telegraphed Chairman Huang Shaoxiong yesterday, saying, "To Chairman Huang Shaoxiong of the Zhejiang Provincial Government: The people of Zhejiang have suffered for a long time. We are delighted that you have come to Zhejiang to govern, and your benevolent reputation has spread, and we are all celebrating the restoration. Tracing the reasons why our people are suffering, it is due to the double oppression of natural disasters and man-made disasters, and the heavy surcharges on land taxes are the burden that our people cannot bear. The heavier the tax amount, the more the arrears, leading to the tragic situation of official and civilian difficulties today. Zhejiang Province has always been known for the heaviest tax amount. In recent years, the implementation of various new policies has all been taken from the surcharges on land taxes. Year after year, there has been an increase without a decrease, especially the increase of one yuan per tael of special construction donation and one yuan per stone of compensation gold. It is understood that this special donation was originally a military special donation. During the Northern Expedition in the 17th year of the Republic of China, in order to support the completion of unification, the people of Zhejiang did not dare to object. Later, the original plan was changed, and it was renamed as a special construction donation, and continued to be levied. The people have repeatedly opposed it, and our association has repeatedly asked for its abolition in accordance with the Ministry of Finance's regulations on reorganizing land tax surcharges and the order to abolish exorbitant taxes and miscellaneous taxes. However, it was used as a fund for reorganizing debts and was not approved. Now, I read in the Southeast Daily in Hangzhou on November 22 this year that the Ministry of Finance replied to the Provincial Government, and stated in the document on reducing the special construction donation that the Provincial Government listed a list of 3 to 4 million yuan on August 16 this year. This special donation has not yet reached the expiration date of the original case, and a preliminary reduction has been made from the balance of the debt fund. It shows that the people of Zhejiang are suffering, and the so-called debt fund now has a surplus, so this special donation should be reduced, which will not hinder the government's credit. In the midst of the drought, a reduction of one cent of burden for the people will leave one cent of vitality. Our association is deeply concerned that the provincial treasury is empty and does not dare to ask for a complete abolition. We only ask you to refer to the Ministry's consultation and temporarily reduce half of it, as a sign of your benevolence and love for the people. We hope you will investigate and implement the case. The All-Zhejiang Association in Shanghai kowtows."

People's Whereabouts Log 156

Zhang Jingjiang, Zhu Jiahua, and Ma Chaojun took the night express train to Beijing yesterday

Yang Hu Discusses the Aftermath of the Tongfu Ship 157

Listing Points in Three Sections

Following the sinking of the Tongan Company's Tongan ship in Korean waters, the Chinese Seamen's Special Party Department, acting on a request from the relief committee organized by various seamen's groups, repeatedly negotiated with the company. Zhuo Huimin, the responsible party from the company, entrusted lawyer Zhang Henghai to allocate 1,200 yuan as an initial payment for the families of the deceased. However, no final settlement has been reached regarding compensation. According to a statement by standing committee member Yang Hu, the matter is divided into three points, as follows: (1) Because Bao Anfu, the manager of Tongan Company, went to Japan to collect insurance money but has not returned, the families of the deceased have been stranded in Shanghai for a long time. The living expenses issued to each person are only twenty or thirty yuan, and many of the families have come from remote villages, with thin clothing and in a state of hunger and cold, which is very pitiful. It is hoped that Zhuo Huimin, the responsible representative, will resolve the issue of compensation for the families of the deceased as soon as possible in accordance with regulations, to console the dead and reassure the living. Otherwise, I will have to advocate for strict negotiations in my official capacity to prompt the company to realize its responsibilities. (2) Navigation workers are originally the productive elements of the company, and the company should pay attention to protecting their lives and safety, or take out seaman's insurance on their behalf. When necessary, both parties can benefit. (3) At the same time, regarding the equipment on each ship, I sincerely hope that the competent authorities will pay close attention to it, striving for perfection to reduce the danger to navigation workers and prevent the unfortunate incident of the Tongfu ship from happening again. Because Tongan Company's equipment is simple and it has not joined the Shipowners' Association, it is difficult to achieve the effect of mutual encouragement among peers, so its measures are difficult to meet the requirements.

Harvard Ship Sinking: Salvage Abandoned 158

Half of the Foreign Rice Recovered Yesterday

After the Harvard ship, which was sunk in the Huangpu River after a collision, the Jianghai Customs notified the shipowner to salvage it within a time limit and to pay 100,000 yuan in cash to the customs as a salvage deposit. After discussion by the shipowner, it was decided to abandon the salvage because the cost of raising the ship's hull was too high, and it would have to be repaired again in the future, which was not cost-effective. The 100,000 yuan will also not be paid to the customs. If the shipowner does not proceed with the salvage, the ship will be disposed of by the Jianghai Customs, and the shipowner will have no right to interfere. The ship has water insurance of 120,000 yuan, so the shipowner will not suffer a major loss in fact.

After the Shanghai Management Office hired eighteen divers to enter the water for salvage, 7,500 bags of foreign rice in various cabins of the ship had been recovered by yesterday morning, but all were stained with water. Half of the rice is still on the ship and will have to be salvaged again at the beginning of the new year.

The Hydrographic Bureau of the Navy Department specially issued Announcement No. 179, stating that a sunken ship occurred at the Shanghai port of the Yangtze River estuary, and a signal marking the sunken ship was established to alert all ships. The location of the sunken ship is in the fourth section of the Huangpu River, 139 degrees north from the tide observation point in the park, at a distance of 2.2 chains, which is 121 degrees 29 minutes east longitude and 31 degrees 14 minutes north latitude. The upper part of the sunken Harvard ship is exposed above the water. The location of the sunken ship on the chart should be marked with the symbol for "exposed at low tide." The above position is the location of the stern of the sunken ship, and the direction of the ship's hull extends 260 feet from that point at 29 degrees north. The marking signals are on the foremast and stern flagpole, with two constantly illuminated vertical green and white lights at night (green above white), and a green flag displayed during the day. Because a part of the ship's hull extends into the waterway, all passing ships must be extra careful to avoid endangering the salvage work. All ships should pass to the west of the sunken ship.

Social Affairs Bureau Orders All Organizations to Follow Procedures When Interpreting Laws and Regulations 163

The Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau yesterday instructed various organizations in the city, stating that the Municipal Government's Order No. 11387 states: "The Ministry of Industry and Commerce's Business Letter No. 29262 states that if agricultural associations, labor unions, fishermen's associations, chambers of commerce, and industrial and commercial guilds have doubts about relevant laws and regulations, they should submit a request for interpretation to avoid errors. However, the submission procedures should first be submitted to the local competent authorities for review and instruction. If they are unable to answer, the competent authorities should add detailed opinions based on the law and local facts and forward them for review and handling. Recently, it has been found that the above organizations often directly submit requests for interpretation of laws and regulations to the Ministry, or the wording is too simple, or the meaning is obscure, or even chapters and clauses are cut apart, and facts are concealed, in order to obtain a favorable interpretation to use as a tool to deal with the other party. Various malpractices are inevitable. For the sake of prudence, the Ministry requires that all organizations must follow the above procedures when submitting requests for interpretation of laws and regulations and must not directly submit them to the Ministry. All competent authorities should first review such cases. If there are indeed doubts, they should forward them to ensure brevity and prudence. In addition to separate consultations, it is appropriate to consult for compliance, etc." It is ordered that the bureau forward these instructions for compliance.

Re-Trial of Xue Baorun's Grandson's Property Dispute Case 169

Hua Yihong is Unwilling to Participate

Declares Abandonment in Court

Hua Lihou, the son-in-law of the late paint tycoon Xue Baorun, believes that his wife also had the right to inherit the millions of dollars of property left by his father-in-law. Although his wife passed away early, she gave birth to two sons, Yihong and Yigu, and a daughter, Manyun, who can inherit in her place. Later, because Yihong expressed his unwillingness to inherit the property, Hua Lihou, as the legal representative of Yigu and Manyun only, hired a lawyer to file a lawsuit against Xue Baorun's sons Xue Gansheng, Yansheng, Jiasheng, Gensheng, and Kunzhong to divide the estate. After two trials by the First Special District District Court and the Second Branch of the High Court, Hua won the lawsuit. However, the Xue brothers were very dissatisfied and appealed to the Supreme Court for a third trial, hoping to win the final victory. The lawsuit has been going on for two years and has not yet been concluded. Recently, after review by the Supreme Court, it was deemed that the previous judgments were not thorough enough, and the entire case was returned to the Second Branch of the High Court for a new trial. Yesterday afternoon, the Civil Division Chief Li Dong and two judges, Ye and Cai, specially convened a collegiate bench to summon both parties and the main witness Hua Yihong for questioning. According to Yihong's testimony, Yigu is my younger brother, Manyun is my younger sister, and Xue Gansheng and others are all my maternal uncles. I am unwilling to participate in this lawsuit of my younger siblings against my maternal uncles. Because my maternal grandfather and maternal grandmother treated me very well, I do not want to divide their property. Moreover, a man should be self-reliant and should not rely on inheritance. Even if my younger siblings win the lawsuit in the future and divide the property, I will never covet it. Even if they want to divide what they have obtained equally with me, I am still willing to abandon it and not accept it. I have this ambition and will never change it. Judge Li pointed out that the word "abandon" has two meanings: one is to abandon the claim to the right of inheritance from the Xue family, and the other is to abandon the claim to divide the property obtained from the analysis with Hua Yigu. Judge Li asked Yihong to make a clearer statement about which aspect he was abandoning. Yihong immediately stated without hesitation that he was abandoning his claim against his maternal uncles and was unwilling to participate in the lawsuit from beginning to end. The court verified the testimony. Because the lawyer representing the defendants Hua Yigu et al. filed a motion for postponement, the court adjourned the hearing to a later date.

Zhang Guoxun's Father's Land Deed Lawsuit Awaits Judgment 170

Supreme Court Remands for Retrial

After the sports figure Zhang Guoxun married Ms. Zhu Qiaozhen, his father, Zhang Xietang, felt that he had a good son and daughter-in-law who would take care of him and entrusted them with the management of the family affairs. He handed over all the family property and deeds to Guoxun for safekeeping, including a land deed. Later, Zhu Qiaozhen took the deed away, and the monthly rent was also collected by her for eight or nine years. Last year, Guoxun and Zhu suddenly fell out and filed a lawsuit in court, requesting a divorce. However, after three trials, it was ruled that Guoxun's claims were not sufficient to constitute grounds for divorce, and his lawsuit was rejected. Guoxun, unable to get a divorce, became even more resentful. He asked Zhu to return the land deed, but she claimed that her father-in-law Xietang owed a certain lumber company 6,000 taels of silver in mortgage. She borrowed money from her brother to repay the debt, and the deed was handed over to her brother for safekeeping as collateral. She refused to return it. Guoxun discussed the matter with his father, Xietang, who then filed a lawsuit against his son and daughter-in-law, requesting the return of the land deed, claiming that the deed was originally handed over to Guoxun for safekeeping, but now he is old and his son and daughter-in-law do not support him. He requested a judgment ordering the return of the land deed and the rent collected over the years. After two trials by the First Special District District Court and the Second Branch of the High Court, Xietang lost the lawsuit. He was dissatisfied and appealed to the Supreme Court. Recently, the Supreme Court remanded the case to the Second Branch of the High Court, instructing them to re-examine the following two points: (1) How did the disputed land deed come into Zhu Qiaozhen's possession? (2) How did Zhu Qiaozhen hand over the deed to her brother? Therefore, the branch court specially opened a hearing yesterday afternoon. Zhang Xietang's representative lawyer, Wu Linkun, detailed the dispute, stating that the land deed was taken away by Zhu Qiaozhen privately, as Guoxun had already testified. Although Zhu claimed that she borrowed money from her brother to repay the mortgage debt and handed over the deed to her brother, there was no evidence to prove it. It was suspected that the brother and sister colluded to embezzle the land. It was requested to abandon the original judgment and order the return of the original deed. Zhu Qiaozhen's lawyer claimed that the handing over of the deed to her brother as collateral for the loan was agreed upon by Zhang and his son. After mutual debate, Judge Li adjourned the hearing for a scheduled judgment.

Zhao Baoshan Sentenced to Two Years in Prison and Fined 3,000 Yuan

Ren Sida's Appeal is Rejected and Still Sentenced to One Year

Yang Jianping, who defected in the Minbian Incident and served as the director of the Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau, colluded with Zhao Baoshan to inflate the price of land purchased by the bureau and divide the profits equally. Liu Shufan, who succeeded Yang, and Ren Sida, the manager of the Shanghai Savings and Remittance Branch, were also accused of using the name of Daixunji to embezzle bureau funds to purchase government bonds, all of which were acts that harmed the national treasury. The Procuratorate of the First Special District District Court prosecuted the case according to law. The Criminal Division of the same court sentenced Liu and others to imprisonment ranging from one year to two and a half years. All defendants were dissatisfied and appealed to the Second Branch of the High Court. Among them, Zou Yu and Liu Shifang, the defense lawyers of Liu Shufan and Yang Peichang, submitted detailed reasons for appeal, stating the facts of the case and arguing that the sentences imposed in the first trial were inappropriate and requesting a reversal. The prosecuting prosecutor also appealed, arguing that the sentences imposed in the first trial were too lenient. After repeated hearings and investigations by the Second Branch of the High Court, Judge Yu, together with Judges Zhao and Zhou, took their seats yesterday afternoon and announced the judgment. The sentences in the original judgment regarding Liu Shufan, Yang Peichang, and Zhao Baoshan were all revoked. Liu Shufan and Yang Peichang were both declared not guilty. Zhao Baoshan was sentenced to two years in prison and fined 3,000 yuan. If he chose to commute the fine to imprisonment, three yuan would be offset for one day of imprisonment, and the imprisonment period could not exceed one year. He was also deprived of public rights for five years. The other appeals of the prosecutor and Ren Sida's appeal were rejected. Therefore, Ren Sida must still be sentenced to one year of imprisonment according to the original trial, and the sentence will be executed after it is finalized.

A Husband's Misconduct Leads to Wife's Petition for Legal Separation 175

Mediation Fails, Formal Lawsuit to Follow

Xu Liangqi, a local resident of 52 Wenlin Road in the French Concession, is 27 years old. His parents are deceased, leaving him with over 100,000 taels of gold in fields and property. When his parents were alive, he was betrothed through a matchmaker to Ms. Xu (age 29), the daughter of Xu Zhitian, a fellow villager from the western Xu Jia Hui Catholic Church. They married in 1924. Initially, the couple's love was strong, lasting over a decade, and they had three sons and one daughter. Unexpectedly, after his mother's death, Xu began living off his inheritance. His attitude changed abruptly, and he started wandering about, squandering his wealth, leaving little remaining. His wife repeatedly劝劝 him, but he refused to listen. He then became acquainted with a Ms. Tang, residing at 19 Tianyou Lane, Haige Road, and began cohabiting with her. They have since had a child together. Xu wanted to bring Ms. Tang home to marry her, but Ms. Xu refused, leading to a breakdown in the couple's relationship. Quarrels became frequent, even leading to violence, with Xu beating his wife. Unable to endure the abuse any longer, Ms. Xu took her children and sought refuge with relatives. She retained lawyer Wang Shizong to file a petition with the Civil Mediation Office of the Special Second District Court, requesting mediation for a legal separation from her husband. The petition stated that she married Xu Liangqi on the 19th day of the 12th month of the lunar calendar in 1924, and for 11 years, they lived in peace and had children: Changhua, currently five years old; Xiangen, four years old; Sanmao, two years old; and Yinlin, eight years old. This year, however, the petitioner has been frequently beaten by the respondent for no reason, and she reported the injuries to the police. After mediation by relatives Xu Zhou, Xu Zitian, Xu Xiaoyan, Xu Yougen, and Yao Jinxiang, they reconciled. On October 23rd of this year, a written agreement was made, stipulating that neither party should have affairs or engage in improper conduct, and that both parties should uphold proper behavior and refrain from further abuse. However, after the agreement was signed, the respondent continued to beat the petitioner and threaten to kill her. He also took money and turned off the lights, dismissing the tenants to avoid being seen. The petitioner dared not return home. The respondent spends his days and nights away from home. It has recently been discovered that he is cohabiting with Tang Bao Bao, the daughter of Tang A’xian, at 19 Tianyou Lane, Haige Road. They had a child on the 28th day of the 10th month of the lunar calendar. He maliciously abandoned the petitioner and intends to bring Tang Bao Bao home, demanding day and night that the petitioner move out and let him do as he pleases. Her aunt Xu Zhou can testify to this. Such circumstances constitute a violation of the reconciliation agreement. According to Articles 3 and 4, it is impossible to continue living together, and her life is in danger. Therefore, she has no choice but to request a separation, with the children under her care. All assets should be divided equally to avoid waste, ensuring that the children's education and living expenses are covered in the future, and that the petitioner's life can be temporarily sustained. The court approved the petition. Yesterday, Judge Tu Shenjie of the Civil Court convened a hearing for mediation. The petitioner and her lawyer attended, recounting the situation. As the respondent Xu Liangqi did not appear, the official ruled that mediation was unsuccessful and instructed that a formal lawsuit be filed.

Animal Disease Prevention Center to Prevent Foot-and-Mouth Disease Outbreak 178

The Disease Has Been Found in Livestock Within the City

A Large-Scale Inspection Will Be Conducted

Foot-and-mouth disease is a livestock ailment. Once discovered, domestic animals such as cattle, sheep, and pigs are at risk of infection, and it can even affect humans, spreading rapidly and posing a significant danger. The disease originates from a filterable microorganism, difficult to see even with the highest-powered microscope. It is present in the saliva, tears, nasal discharge, feces, blood, milk, and muscles of infected animals. If other livestock become contaminated, infection is possible. Even-toed ungulates, such as cattle, sheep, and pigs, are most susceptible, especially cattle, followed by pigs and sheep. After infection, symptoms appear in about one to seven days. Initially, body temperature rises to around 40 degrees Celsius, appetite decreases, and milk production suddenly drops. After one or two days, blisters appear on the oral mucosa, the back and tip of the tongue, the inside of the cheeks, gums, and tip of the nose. Body temperature decreases to normal levels. After another three or four days, the blisters rupture, and the epidermis peels off. In addition to the oral symptoms, the coronary band, interdigital space, and teats of the infected animals also become hot, followed by blisters that rupture. The hooves develop ulcerated lesions, making walking difficult. In mild cases, recovery is expected within two to three weeks. In severe cases, death occurs in a few days. While the mortality rate is low in mild cases, the loss to the dairy industry is enormous. The mortality rate in severe cases is very high, over 70 percent. If infants are infected, they develop malignant enteritis. According to reports from veterinarians at the Animal Disease Prevention Center (jointly operated by the Ministry of Industry's Central Agricultural Experiment Station and the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau), foot-and-mouth disease has been found in livestock in Shanghai, most commonly in yellow cattle and water buffalo, and is gradually affecting dairy cattle. The outbreak is most prevalent in the southern city and Zhabei, accounting for about 50 percent. Fortunately, it is a mild case, and the mortality rate is low. To prevent and eradicate the disease, the center has held two meetings with the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau, the Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau, and the Public Concession Bureau's veterinarians. It has been decided to conduct a large-scale inspection. It is hoped that people from all walks of life will strictly guard against the disease in all kinds of livestock. All milk and meat should be cooked before consumption to prevent infection. If any livestock are infected, the above agencies should be notified immediately for guidance and assistance with disinfection. The center has printed a pamphlet titled "Important Information on Foot-and-Mouth Disease in Shanghai," providing detailed instructions, which has been distributed to milk parlors and related agencies. The center has also submitted reports on the epidemic situation and prevention measures to the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau and the Central Agricultural Experiment Station, which will be forwarded to the Ministry of Industry and distributed to various provinces for inspection and prevention. Veterinarians have been dispatched to Jiangsu and Anhui to investigate and determine prevention strategies.

Fire at Iron Factory Due to Oil Stove Pipe Leak Kills Six, Injures Two 180

Four Dead...Two Injured in Critical Condition

Zhao Jinyuan, a local resident, 42 years old, residing at 43 Lane 4, Oujia Road, Zhoujiazui Road, Hongkou, runs a machinery iron factory. Therefore, he opened the Zhao Jinji Machinery Iron Factory downstairs in his residence, employing dozens of workers. Yesterday morning, around 7:10 AM, six workers were rushing to manufacture military water bottles. They used an air pump stove to produce the outer shells of the water bottles in front of the motor room. Unexpectedly, the oil stove pipe suddenly leaked, causing the oil to shoot out and splash onto the motor engine, causing an immediate fire. The fire spread rapidly, quickly reaching all around the building. Smoke and flames spread everywhere, making it impossible to control. At that time, the six workers who were working tried to put out the fire, but to no avail. They were overcome by smoke and fell unconscious in the motor room. As the fire raged, the motor room had only one door for entry and exit, making it impossible to put out the fire inside. Fortunately, the Central Fire Brigade received a warning and rushed fire trucks to the scene to extinguish the flames. They broke through the wall to drag out the six workers. Four of them had already been burned to death, and two were severely burned. Firefighters worked hard to save the other houses upstairs and downstairs, preventing the fire from spreading. After about two hours, the fire was completely extinguished, but the motor room was completely destroyed. The two injured workers, Yao Yongxin, 20 years old, from Suzhou, and Zhu Tianrong, 19 years old, from Changzhou, were rushed to the hospital by ambulance. Their injuries were severe, and their lives were in danger. The four workers who were burned to death were Qi Xiaopei, 17 years old, from Liyang; Mao Rongkang, 21 years old, from Changzhou; Shen Xiliang, 21 years old, from Wuxi; and Huang Jinhai, 15 years old, from Chongming. The fire truck sent the bodies to the morgue for autopsy. The Jiading Road Police Station also sent officers to investigate and file a report for questioning.

Public Concession Increases Winter Security Forces 181

The Shanghai Chinese Ratepayers' Association previously received a letter from the United Association of Citizens of the First Special District, requesting notification to the Public Concession to increase security forces. Shallow Winter Water Levels Hinder Inland Waterways Navigation 182

Zhenze Water Levels Low

Old Wharf Blocked

Recently, due to the winter season, water levels in waterways everywhere are low, making it difficult for ships to travel, especially smaller boats to Huzhou. Recently, small boats from Shanghai to Huzhou, and boats towed by companies, are unable to pass once they reach Zhenze due to the shallow water. Various shipping companies in Zhenze City have recently dispatched shallow-draft civilian boats to transfer goods and passengers to avoid disrupting transportation. However, after passing the difficult shallow channel of Zhenze, the waterway is often blocked by cement and gravel boats near Old Wharf, about 30 to 40 li from Huzhou, sometimes preventing passage for an entire day. This often causes delays in Huzhou-bound boats. Inland waterway bureaus have requested that authorities take measures to clear the cement and gravel boats (many of which are hired by cement factories to transport stone for mud).

The National Goods Industry, recognizing that small industrial manufacturers are only concerned with profits, often producing substandard products, believes that this will inevitably lead to a loss of customer confidence and significantly impact the future of the national goods industry. Therefore, they are actively gathering manufacturers to discuss remedial measures. After two meetings, in addition to notifying each industry to strive for high-quality manufacturing, they are also conducting detailed investigations of each manufacturer's production and sales volumes to prepare for the second step of rescue measures.

Telegraph Bureau Specifies New Method for Change in Telegram Fees 187

Change for amounts of 5 cents or less can be paid in auxiliary currency; above that, change can be given.

For amounts of 1 cent or less, postage stamps can be used for payment.

Since the Shanghai Telegraph Bureau implemented the method of calculating telegram fee change according to postal rates from December, as ordered by the Ministry of Communications, it has been two decades. However, the volume of telegrams at the bureau is enormous. Besides the telegram fees that are whole numbers in national currency, the rest all involve change. Since the implementation of the new method, senders of telegrams almost always pay for telegram fees in silver dollars and demand change from the telegraph bureau, requiring the bureau to prepare a large amount of subsidiary currency notes for change every day. In recent days, subsidiary currency notes have been exceptionally scarce in the market. Therefore, the bureau has specially stipulated three new methods: (1) For telegram fees of 5 cents or less, the sender shall pay the subsidiary currency according to the exchange rate announced by the post office (including silver dimes, dime notes, and copper coins, etc.). (2) For telegram fees of 5 cents and 1 point or more, if the sender pays in silver dollars and requests change, the bureau shall pay the subsidiary currency according to the exchange rate announced by the post office (including silver dimes, dime notes, and copper coins, etc.). (3) For amounts of 1 cent or less, if the sender uses postage stamps or is willing to accept postage stamps instead of copper coins for change, it shall be handled accordingly. The above methods shall be uniformly implemented from the 29th of this month. Yesterday, it has also been announced to all receiving and dispatching offices for general knowledge.

The Poor Children's Meeting sponsored by the Shanghai YMCA, after a long period of preparation, was held yesterday morning in eleven locations. This event was a pioneering effort, but it achieved such great results that it will be a good model for those who continue to organize such events in the future, making it easy to solve problems.

Lu Lishi's 15-year-old daughter, Xiuying, a resident of a bungalow on Guangxin Road, had been a worker at the Yufeng Yarn Factory in Yangshupu. Sentenced to Six Months Imprisonment

Jiang Shenshi, a woman from Shaoxing, was recently secretly selling the narcotic drug "red pills" in her house at 143 Dongjiaxing Road for profit. Chinese detective Yin Xingsheng discovered this and secretly went to arrest her at the address, seizing 705 narcotic pills. She was taken to the Jiaxing Road Police Station and transferred to the women's prison. Yesterday, she was brought before the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. Public Concession lawyer Li Zhishan stated that her husband, Jiang Xiaojinlin, had previously been sentenced to one year imprisonment for the same offense. He requested that the defendant be prosecuted for continuing to engage in this illegal behavior. The red pills were presented for inspection. When questioned, she gave evasive answers and denied that they were hers. Judge Wu Zehan sentenced Jiang Shenshi to six months imprisonment, and the evidence was confiscated.

The French police recently discovered that Liu Jinbao, at 29 Ningfu Lane, Glock Road, was selling morphine. Prohibition of Newspaper Deliverymen Demanding Tips for Drinks 202

Notice from the Telegraph and Cable Bureaus

The Shanghai Telegraph Bureau of the Ministry of Communications and the International Telegraph Bureau, regarding the matter of newspaper deliverymen demanding tips for drinks, hereby issue a notice to all sectors: It has been found that newspaper deliverymen from our bureau and others are demanding tips for drinks, which has always been a prohibited practice. We have repeatedly published notices to this effect. As the end of the year approaches, we are concerned that some unscrupulous individuals may violate these regulations. We hereby reiterate to all sectors that if any such situation occurs, please identify the deliveryman's number and report it to our bureau for investigation and punishment. We hope for your understanding.

Liu Boyan Holds Solo Exhibition 204

Drawing on Lots Today at the Lili Art Company on Sijing Road

The Shu region is rich in talent. For example, Su Dongpo of the Song dynasty and Zhang Chuanshan of the Qing dynasty were all masters of poetry, calligraphy, and painting, celebrated in the art world and passed down to later generations. Recently, the Daqian brothers, famous painters in Shanghai, have also been praised as the "Double Ding and Two Lu." It can be proven that the spiritual energy of Mount Emei is always bestowed upon someone in each generation. The young painter Liu Boyan possesses such talent. Five or six years ago, he was an outstanding student at the Changming Art School. While still in school, he attracted the attention of professors Wang Yiting, He Tianjian, Wang Geyi, and Wu Dongmai. Since graduating, he has worked even harder and devoted himself to studying the styles of the Song and Yuan dynasties. His art has become increasingly refined. Those who once noticed him are now full of praise. Boyan, however, remains humble and self-disciplined, focusing on his studies and immersing himself in fundamental learning. Therefore, his works, including flowers, plants, figures, birds, fruits, and vegetables, are both meticulous and expressive, resembling ancient masterpieces and completely devoid of current trends. He is truly a rising talent in the modern art world. He will soon exhibit his finest works at a solo exhibition at the Lili Art Company on Sijing Road on the 26th of this month. It is said that most of the pieces have already been reserved. Art connoisseurs and fellow artists who admire his talent are vying to visit, promising a grand occasion.

Post Office Revises Regulations for Sending International Mail 208

Effective January 1st of Next Year

Shanghai Postal Administration Notice No. 1187 states: In accordance with the International Postal Convention, effective January 1st of next year, the ordinary postage for documents in Braille or embossed script for the blind sent abroad will be reduced from 5 cents to 3 cents per kilogram. The minimum postage per item will also be reduced from 5 cents to 3 cents. Also, starting on the same date, the size limit for letters sent abroad will be changed to a combined length, width, and thickness of 90 centimeters, with the largest side not exceeding 60 centimeters. For rolled items, twice the diameter plus the length must not exceed 100 centimeters, and the largest side must not exceed 80 centimeters. In addition, the size limit for newspapers, books, printed matter, commercial papers, samples, and documents in Braille or embossed script for the blind sent abroad will be the same as for letters sent abroad. This notice is hereby issued to ensure that the public is aware of the changes.

A Summary of the Assassination Year of 1934 220

— He Shanggong

The calendar for 1934 is running out of pages. In the world, 1934 can be called the "Year of Assassinations." Now, let's open a summary account.

(1) Dollfuss Austrian Chancellor Dollfuss was known as the "Little Napoleon" in Europe. In July, he was assassinated by members of the Austrian Nazi Party. People, mindful of the eve of the outbreak of World War I in 1916, which also began with the assassination of Archduke Franz Ferdinand, believed that a spark could ignite an unprecedented catastrophe. It was thought that the old feud between Germany and France, with Germany trying to succeed in the Danube River basin and expand its influence to Southern Europe, Austria would bear the brunt. Italy, France, England, and Russia did not want Austria to be incorporated into Germany, making Austria a buffer zone. Therefore, after Dollfuss's death, Italy stationed troops on the border, observing the situation closely. Whether Germany was really behind this incident is still in question today.

(2) Alexander King Alexander I of Yugoslavia was traveling to Marseille by car on October 9. Amid a grand welcome, a killer, Kalman, suddenly drew a pistol and shot at the king. King Alexander was shot four times and died instantly. This was the "Marseille Massacre" that shocked the world. It is said that Kalman was a member of the Ustasha terrorist party. Some say it was an ethnic struggle, but it actually had serious international implications. Now, this matter has reached the League of Nations. In order to appease the situation, the League of Nations will conclude an international convention to crack down on terrorist acts. Hungary has also denied expelling Yugoslavian overseas Chinese, and Germany has also advocated German-French friendship. Hopefully this is the end of it, and the opportunity for the outbreak of war will not be promoted further.

(3) Barthou French Foreign Minister Barthou was also killed by a bullet, because he used himself to shield King Alexander. Barthou, a central figure in European politics for the past decade, became a victim alongside King Alexander. At the same time, Geneva also lost an important figure. He was a very astute and eloquent politician, and also an author. His assassination is not only a loss to France, but also a loss to Europe.

(4) Shi Liangcai The assassination of Mr. Shi Liangcai, general manager of Shen Bao, is considered a major loss to Chinese society, even acknowledged by foreigners. But, the body is mortal, the spirit is immortal. May Mr. Shi rest in peace!

(5) Kirov The assassination of Kirov, a member of the Central Executive Committee of the Soviet Union, on December 1, was this the end of the assassination cases of 1934?
