Shenbao Local Supplement Movie Special

"Blindness to Mount Tai" Movie Stars are Hard to Recognize 311

— Fine Stream

Do you think that you can always recognize your favorite movie stars at a glance? Well, think again.

Not long ago, a large group of deeply addicted movie fans went to Hollywood for a tour. A large company had provided them with a special guide! | As usual, a smooth-talking handsome young man | | was leading them, touring various parts of the company. Soon they arrived in front of a star's dressing room. There was a shiny black car parked there, and a chauffeur was sitting inside waiting. After a while, a woman strode past the large group of tourists, brushed past them, and jumped into the car and drove away. The large group of tourists didn't even give the woman in trousers and tousled hair a second look. Guess who she was? She was none other than the Swedish actress Greta Garbo, the one the star-hunting group wanted to capture and the fans most wanted to find! They watched her walk past with their eyes wide open. If they had recognized her, would she have been able to calmly get into the car and escape? What's most strange is that even the young guide from the company didn't recognize her. He later told people privately that he had been at the company for many years, but he had never seen Greta Garbo. But had he really not seen her? Or did he see her but not recognize her?

Therefore, I advise my friends not to casually bet that you can recognize movie stars at a glance, or that you can recognize Charlie Chaplin from afar as easily as a sailor recognizes a lighthouse. Once, a large circus troupe went to Hollywood, and Chaplin took his two children to see the circus. He and his two children sat together in the front row, eating peanuts and talking and laughing. He didn't wear his little mustache, nor did he wear a bowler hat, nor did he carry a small cane, nor did he wear broken boots and torn pants. He sat and watched the show peacefully, and no one in the audience recognized him. Who would have known that he was the comedian worshiped by millions?

Even in the famous restaurants of Hollywood, where you expect to see many stars, the stars might slip right under your nose without you even realizing it. One day, Sylvia Sidney wore dark glasses and sat in the company's restaurant for lunch. She sat for half a day without anyone recognizing her. Later, George Raft called out her name, and only then did people realize who she was. But after she was discovered, she immediately stood up and ran away. Garbo's clothes are also very ordinary, not attracting anyone's attention at all. Once, a naval officer went to a company to buy white canvas trousers. At the same time, a woman was also buying the same thing. The friend deliberately cut in front of the woman to buy them and deliberately took his time picking them out, making her wait a while longer. When he finished buying them and was about to leave, he realized that the woman was none other than the famous Greta Garbo. He had unintentionally made her wait for half a day.

Female stars are more difficult to recognize than male stars. It is said that the spots on a leopard will not change. But women are the best at changing. The Chinese say that a daughter changes eighteen times, and three more times before getting into the sedan chair. Now, Hollywood female stars only need to change their hairstyle, wear old clothes, and put on dark glasses, and you simply can't tell who they are. Moreover, there are so many people imitating each female star. They also wear old clothes and put on dark glasses, making it impossible for you to tell who is the real star and who is the fake star. When Anna Sten goes out, her face is covered in powder. Her hair is tousled, peeking out from under her small hat. When you see her, you just think she is a pretty female student from a nearby school. Mae West also doesn't wear diamonds. She wears long pants and a sweater. Who would know that she is the glamorous superstar who has caused a sensation across the country? Jean Harlow is especially difficult to recognize because there are too many people imitating her. Many extras who dress up as Jean Harlow look more like her than she does herself. And the number of platinum blonde women is increasing day by day, but there is only one real platinum blonde woman. Years ago, Gloria Swanson deliberately put on a set of old clothes, styled her hair differently, and went to several of her companies looking for work. She said her name was Rochelle Gray. She went to several companies, but none of them were willing to hire her. They all said she didn't look fashionable. At that time, Gloria was at the height of her popularity, but when she wore old clothes, no one recognized her.

In addition, a female star must have several doubles - people whose appearance is similar to the lead actor, used by the company to replace the star when necessary, and also to intimidate the star, so that she does not dare to be too stubborn. These doubles, walking on the street, are taken by autograph seekers as the real stars. When they see the real stars, they think they are fake.

Film Review

Review of "Flying Flower Village" 312

— Ling He, Tang Na

"Flying Flower Village," as an exposé film, shows progress in the expression of the author of "Spring Tide." The distance between the love elegy of "Spring Tide" and the exposure of the darkness of society in "Flying Flower Village" is very far. Every petty-bourgeois author is often like this. He feels great interest in the sorrow and joy of love. But after the cruel reality constantly hits him, the pink dreams cannot but slowly disappear, and then he is forced to embark on a positive path. That is to say, he faces reality to a certain extent, and his work reflects dissatisfaction and anger with the current social situation.

Very clearly, in "Spring Tide," the author unfolded the disillusionment of love. Wang Renmei hoped to obtain perfect love (since the names of the characters in the play have been forgotten, the names of the actors will be used temporarily). Gao Zhanfei was also very passionate, but he could not withstand the attack of Li Li, the demon of lust, which destroyed their love, and their lives died with their love. So the author cried and sang, "Sweet dreams, come back!" But that dream will never return. The tragedy of love unfolds there, but it is only the tragedy of love, and it does not transcend the scope of love to exist as a positive reflection of social reality. However, the sweet dreams of love are indeed destroyed for the author. In the second work, "Flying Flower Village," he tossed away the illusions of love, and in the flower-selling voices of the village women, the ugliness of the stationmaster and other noble people was revealed. They were hungry for lust and privately trafficked in contraband. On the other hand, the flower-selling girls played by Hu Ping, when they still have to work hard to live, they have no possibility of working, and they cannot live except by selling their bodies, let alone relieve the poverty of their husbands and daughters. The adoption of such a theme and the determination of the theme do have some positive progress compared to "Spring Tide."

However, the author is still very interested in women, in so-called love and desire, so he decided that Hu Ping should take flower-selling as a profession, and flowers and women are always reluctant to separate. Similarly, a lot of film was spent on the scenery of the salted meat shop.... These and everything in "Spring Tide" are still very similar. Of course, we are not saying that this kind of material cannot be adopted, but we are using this to illustrate the author's style and tendency.

On the other hand, the author likes tragic creations very much. "Spring Tide" is certainly a tragedy, and in the development of the story of "Flying Flower Village," Hu Ping and Gao Zhanfei may not be able to achieve a relatively complete ending, but he always kills her to complete his tragic ending.

Now, let's see how he expresses it. Like many Chinese works, he adopts a slow TEMPO to express the living habits of Chinese people. However, as a cinematic expression, in the rural and relatively peaceful environment, this slow TEMPO can be applied, but when expressing the city, it feels that a high-speed expression of chaos and annoyance is more appropriate. And the high-speed strengthening of character dynamics is the most cutting-edge expression of the 1930s. From this point of view, the speed of "Flying Flower Village" in the second half is too slow. The most obvious example is when Hu... the police caught Wang Naidong and walked into the courtroom, she did not run at speed, and the slowness of the whole tone is needless to say. Fortunately, the dubbing helped a lot, but it didn't become tense after all.

Secondly, what should be said is that the MONTAGE is not smooth enough. For example, when Gao Zhanfei fought in the train, he was not seen falling on the ground, and then he was connected to the hospital. Also, for example, when Gao Zhanfei hit Hu Ping, people suddenly watched outside the window, which was an improper cut, resulting in a loss of air and insufficient grasp. The parallel development of the other three lines feels chaotic, especially Hu Ping's arrival in the city is described in detail, while Gao Zhanfei's arrival in the city is lightly let go, which shows the author's one-sided concept.

Of course, although there are these shortcomings, they cannot hide the author's efforts. For example, the air of Hanzhuang and the grasp of the personality of the characters in the play have achieved very good results. At the same time, Hu Ping, Gao Zhanfei, Ye Juanjuan, and Wang Naidong are all very good actors. Especially Wang Naidong's calm and experienced acting skills are even more surprising. And Ye Juanjuan, who has never been valued by people, has also achieved very good results here due to the good guidance of the director.

In addition, the efforts of photography and set design have made this film achieve a lot of success. This can also prove that Chinese films are indeed constantly improving in technology. At the end of this 1934, we have high expectations for 1935 due to this film.

Review of "Affairs of Voltaire" 313

— You Jing

The Affairs of Voltaire

- Cathay Release -

Regarding Voltaire, the master of art and literary giant of 18th-century France, I would like to briefly use the following words to explain:

"...Voltaire's philosophical point of view is based on Locke's theory of sensation... It did not have much influence on the development of 18th-century materialism. However, his attacks on Catholicism and court learning, his books of criticism and satire, have special significance. These not only opened up a road for French atheism in the 18th century, but also made great contributions to the revolution. However, he was a "salon" atheist, because he also believed that religion was necessary for the foolish people, it could restrain the barbarous desires of the people, and maintaining the domination of the enlightened old people over the foolish people was a powerful religion. This point shows that his ideo-Voroky is bourgeois aristocratic liberalism."

Voltaire in "Affairs of Voltaire" shown on the screen is a progressive writer with a sense of justice. He cannot stand the absurdity of the Louis XV dynasty and the tyranny of Finance Minister Count Sarnap and others. In the cries and struggles of people starving to death, he sacrificed his weak body for humanity, justice, and freedom, and resolutely wrote pamphlets to shout for the innocent people and write plays exposing the pain of the people and the power of the powerful. He is not afraid of offending the emperor and sycophants. He also did not hesitate to enter hell - the most famous Bastille prison - to spend the darkest and most glorious life with the general enlightened people of the time. However, justice is justice after all, and history, which will not flow backwards, has made the fairest judge. The books that were burned and the bronze statues that were destroyed will eventually be supported and offered by masses of people shouting "bread," "justice," and "freedom."

A slight deficiency is due to the way the playwright handles this great material. He was too concerned about the story of the play's progress, and wrote the queen's respect and belief in Voltaire too mythically. Voltaire's attitude towards Louis and Sarnap was written with a sense of justice greater than the skill of the police, which made us feel like we were seeing the struggle between昏君,奸臣 and loyal and upright prime ministers or censors in Chinese dramas.

Director George Arlen and George Arliss, who played Voltaire, both had great success. The others who played the king, queen, Sarnap, and Miss Nanga did not fail the name of Voltaire. The alertness of the dialogue, the tightness of the weaving, the light photography and sound effects, and the acting skills of each person, etc., unfortunately, this article is limited in length and cannot be described in detail.

Film Novel

The Merry Widow (II) 315

— Su Hua

Sulia lifted a corner of her veil and peeked at Donal from the small window on the stairs, blowing his mouth happily on the path. Only after he jumped over the wall did she lazily stroll back to the bedroom. She changed. She put on her pajamas, walked close to the window facing the garden, and sang softly. At first she just sang softly, but later she couldn't help but sing loudly. Suddenly there was singing outside the garden wall, a man's voice, undoubtedly Donal's.

When the singing stopped, Sulia turned back. She lay on the bed for a while and then said to the maid: "Ask the secretary to find me the address of a person named Donal." But the three maids told her in unison that he lived upstairs at 52 Queen's Road. Sulia blushed and said, "Thank you, that's okay, there's nothing now." The maids said good night to her and went out. Fortunately, she couldn't sleep back and forth on the bed, so she put on her pajamas and got up to open her diary and write urgently. Soon, she finished writing and said happily: "I have written it all out, it will not exist in my heart. I will forget it soon."

The lovely sunshine and warm breeze seemed to keep the things of last night, making Sulia unable to forget. She hoped the days would pass quickly. It was again when the moon was on the willow tips, and she strolled out to the garden again. Sitting on the stone bench, waiting unconsciously. An hour and two hours passed. She walked back dejectedly. She lay on the bed for a while and then went to write her diary. She wrote: "I have forgotten him."

Another day has passed! The moon is still unharmed at night, the garden is still as quiet, and she writes her diary as before before going to bed. But the next day, Sulia was a little different. Thousands of thoughts rushed into her mind aimlessly. She closed all the windows, isolating all happy stimuli. Widowhood and veils can eliminate the entire youth, and the melancholy mood filled her entire soul. The moving songs sung by those soldiers seemed to deliberately penetrate her eardrums through the window gaps. She couldn't bear it anymore. She stood up and pulled the maid's calling cord, hurriedly took out Donal's letter from the drawer and burned it in hatred. She knew, because she knew that all the miserable life could be turned into nothing at the same time as this letter. When the maid came in, all the black clothes were torn to pieces by her. She also shouted in her mouth: "Hurry up and bring me all my new clothes and new things, we will go to Paris tomorrow!"

Sulia's arrival in Paris gave the country of Masovia a great panic. There were constant inquiries about Sulia's actions in Paris. It was said that a certain duke was engaged to her, and it was said that a certain prince was proposing to her. Undoubtedly, Sulia is now a merry widow. The people of Masovia were panicking every day, afraid that she would marry in Paris. Once she gets married, her property in Masovia will not necessarily go with her, and Masovia will go bankrupt. At that time, King Yami wanted to hold a cabinet meeting for this matter, wanting to select a handsome and gentle secret envoy to go to Paris to please the merry widow so that she would not marry a foreigner. Coincidentally, Queen Dorothy and Royal Guard Captain Donal were having a secret meeting at this time, and King Yami caught them. In addition to anger, the king came up with a plan and sent Donal to Paris to meet Ambassador Baff, temporarily acting as the secret envoy of Masovia. As soon as Donal arrived in Paris, his luggage had not been sorted out in the hotel, so he shouted to wear a dress and go to the Maxi dance floor, without even seeing the ambassador. He arrived at Maxi and quarreled with a woman because he kissed a woman, not wanting that person to be Ambassador Baff. Later, the ambassador found out and pulled him into a quiet room and said to him: "This is an important national secret. Give her a dance party at the embassy tomorrow night." Donal deliberately asked: "Is she beautiful?" The ambassador replied: "For her property, she must be beautiful, but whether you like her or not, you must love her. Come to the embassy tomorrow night and I will introduce you to her. Do you think this is a good idea?" Donal excitedly agreed and ran out. (To be continued)

Shen Bao Local Supplement Auto Weekly

Proclamation of Liquidation of French Automobile Giant Citroen 316

— Stagnant

Amid the sounds of recession, British and American automobile factories are expressing that the automobile business in 1934 has entered the path of recovery. However, we cannot deny that the impact of the recession has not been completely restored. Therefore, in the automobile industry in the United Kingdom and the United States, there are indeed many people who can support the facade, and there are also many people who have declared liquidation or mutual merger due to poor turnover. The French automobile business is inherently more backward than the British and American ones, and Citroen is the giant among the domestic automobile factories. However, in the turbulent world of economic recession, this French automobile giant Citroen factory has been heard of for liquidation. It can be seen that the economic crisis is getting worse and worse.

Since the news of the Citroen factory's liquidation was announced, the factory owner Citroen has visited French Prime Minister Florentin to personally present the factory's economic difficulties. At first, the government intended to provide assistance to prevent it from going bankrupt. Citroen factory is a relatively large car factory in France, and it employs a lot of workers. If it goes bankrupt, it will add a batch of unemployed people to France. However, as a result, some members of the council expressed opposition to using government public funds to support private businesses. Therefore, the so-called assistance has become empty talk, and the Citroen factory may be liquidated.

In recent years, the cars produced by Citroen factory have also been improving day by day. And because the French environment is trending towards luxury, Citroen cars are particularly exquisite in the manufacturing of the body. It is said that the 1934 Citroen cars have as many as ninety kinds of body styles. Citroen cars sold in various places are mostly 10 horsepower, large 12 horsepower, and 12 horsepower. In the past year, more than 60,000 of the above three types of vehicles have been sold in various places. Car owners in various places have expressed satisfaction after driving Citroen cars.

In the history of Citroen, the first prize trophies won in exhibitions held in various places have totaled eighteen times. As for the automobile races held in various parts of France, Citroen has also created many top records. Even in international automobile races, according to the official report of the French Automobile Association, Citroen four-cylinder and six-cylinder cars have created 134 French records and 241 world records in France and internationally. The performance of Citroen cars can be seen from this.

Taking the 1934 light 12-horsepower Citroen new car as an example, the maximum speed can reach 68 miles per hour. And it can accelerate from 8 miles per hour to 50 miles per hour in 36 seconds. The rich acceleration is also unmatched by general cars. Acceleration is convenient and easy, and the speed is extremely high. Therefore, car owners who like fast cars buy Citroen cars. The powerful traffic jam, the beautiful appearance, and the heavy chassis are all special advantages of Citroen. Therefore, after the 1934 Citroen new car was launched, it became popular in various places and was welcomed by car owners. Now, this French factory is heard of for liquidation. If it becomes a reality, it will be a great loss to the future of the French automobile industry.

瀛海車訊一束 317

— 頌

The Berlin Auto Show Date is Set. In major cities throughout Europe and America, auto shows are often held at the end of the year and the beginning of the new year. The latest car models are displayed in categories, making it convenient for the public to compare and choose. This excellent practice is also an annual social event. It's like New York in America, London in England, and Paris in France; which one doesn't have an auto show? When the time comes, everyone goes out, creating a feeling of city-wide excitement. The Berlin Auto Show in Germany has now been decided to be held next year. The date has also been chosen, from February 14th to 24th, 1935. The exhibition will last for a total of ten days. In previous years, the Berlin Auto Show venue occupied two large halls. Next year, due to the increase in participating car dealers, the location will also need to be expanded. All halls connected to the large exhibition venue will be used. These halls are connected to the main road through intermediate roads and old halls. It is said that this location is very suitable for vehicle exhibitions. Next year's venue layout will be the same as in previous years. Various types of cars and parts will be divided into several major sections. Therefore, private passenger cars and commercial freight vehicles will be displayed in two separate locations.

London-India Automobile Trip. Recently, Colonel Caillet and his wife, along with two friends, made a long-distance automobile trip between London and India. According to the latest news, their journey is progressing very smoothly. They are using two 27-horsepower Hillman touring cars as their means of transportation. They have now crossed Jerusalem and reached a location near Baghdad. According to their travel diaries, the journey from London to Jerusalem covers a total of 3,423 miles. Their average driving speed is 23 miles per hour. Many places along this route have extremely dry and dusty roads, making it quite difficult to drive. Therefore, under such circumstances, it is not an easy feat for these two Hillman cars to achieve this result.

Innovation at the British Ford Factory. Ford's new-style luxury cars have ample power, beautiful designs, and moderate prices, resulting in supply falling short of demand and a high level of demand. In order to meet the needs and mass production, the Ford factory in Dagenham, England, has specifically renovated and innovated its original car manufacturing plant. In two weeks, the original machinery in the factory, weighing 1,200 pounds, has been disassembled and reassembled. Also, the monorail transport vehicle, which is three-quarters of a mile long, has also been renovated to meet the new production plan. The total investment of the American Ford Company for the new plan in 1935 amounts to £83,000,000. It is estimated that 1,000,000 new cars will be produced in this year.

Goodyear's Java Branch. The American Goodyear Tire & Rubber Company is planning to establish a branch in Buitenzorg, Java. The estimated daily production capacity is 300 rubber outer tires and inner tubes each. The opening date is scheduled for May 1, 1935. At that time, approximately 200 workers will be employed. The factory site is approximately 460 feet long and 200 feet wide, mostly open-style. The building materials are entirely steel, which is most suitable for tropical mechanical factories. The raw material storage room and drying room are all built indoors with windows. The engine and furnace room are separated from most of the factory buildings for safety reasons. The factory site is located on a 28-acre rubber plantation, surrounded by six new-style houses for engineers and management personnel to live in. This Java branch is Goodyear's fifth foreign branch. Their locations are in Canada, England, Australia, and Argentina. As for the original factories, they are in Akron, Ohio, Los Angeles, and Gadsden, Alabama. The head of the Java branch is Mr. Hartley, who has been in the Far East for many years and has abundant experience.

The Sound Suppression Movement Craze in England. The issue of sound suppression is receiving great attention throughout England, especially in bustling cities and metropolises. Local people are making great efforts to maintain public tranquility and are thoroughly seeking a fundamental solution to this issue. The beginning of this matter was initiated by Mr. Hore-Belisha, the Minister of Transport of the British government. There is also a committee, chaired by Sir Henry Fowler, whose members include scientists and manufacturers of automobiles and motorcycles. Their sole objective is to consider and investigate how mechanically propelled vehicles generate unpleasant noise and what methods can be used to eliminate or reduce the production of such noise. On the part of automobile manufacturers, they have spent a lot of effort researching the reduction of automobile noise in recent years. However, there are still many areas to be improved. Recently, it has been learned that the Broadspeed Company in Slough has put a lot of effort into experimenting with sound suppression methods. They are now studying whether asbestos can reduce automobile noise. Asbestos has fireproof and soundproof properties, so it is widely used in modern building construction. Some people advocate using asbestos as a lining for car hoods, especially for old cars. The reason is that the older the car, the louder the noise. If asbestos is used as a lining, then at the very least, it can confine the sound within the hood and prevent it from spreading out.

Pikes Peak Hill Climb Record. The Pikes Peak Hill Climb competition near Colorado Springs, USA, is held annually. Driving in such a venue is indeed a very difficult task. Even without mentioning the record time, just getting the car to ascend to the summit is not an easy task. Circumventing high mountain paths and not facing thousand-foot abysses are all chilling experiences. This year's 16th annual competition was held on American Labor Day. The number of spectators caused traffic congestion. In the open car group, Louis Unser took the top spot with 16 seconds and 18 tenths of a second. He was driving a Green-Goetz Stutz car, surpassing the old championship by nearly a minute. Three Ford V-8 stock cars broke the original stock car record, with Harmon's car having the shortest time, only 19 minutes, 25 and 7 tenths of a second. These drivers were able to achieve such amazing results undoubtedly because of their driving skills and the engine power of the cars. However, one thing that is also worth our attention is that all cars in the open car and stock car groups used Champion spark plugs, which were very effective.

Studebaker Armored Car. At the beginning of last month, the Studebaker factory in South Bend, Indiana, manufactured a fully armored car. This car is a special-made President Eight sedan, prepared for use by the police department. The biggest feature of this car is that it is completely bulletproof. Except for bullets that can penetrate the car from the floor, bullets cannot penetrate from any other direction, such as the roof, front, and sides of the car. This is because the car body is surrounded by bulletproof steel. The windows are made of one-inch-thick bulletproof glass. The windshield also has bulletproof capabilities. As for the four gun ports, they can be closed automatically and are made with rubber clips to prevent the danger of shattering the glass with recoil. The wheels are also protected by bulletproof steel wire in front. The radiator is similarly protected by steel wire, so there is no room for error.
